If her Malone collaboration \"Fortnight\" is victorious, she will break her record to become the only artist to ever three-peat and win five times in the category.\n\nAriana Grande, Eminem and Sabrina Carpenter (6 each); Megan Thee Stallion and SZA (5 each), plus LISA, Olivia Rodrigo and Teddy Swims (4 each) join Swift and Malone as leading nominees.\n\nBenson Boone and Tyla (3 each), Chappell Roan, Rauw Alejandro, Sexyy Red and Victoria Mon\u00e9t (2 each) also received multiple nods. Other first-time nominees include Alexander Stewart, Burna Boy, Coco Jones, Flyana Boss, Gracie Abrams, Gunna, Joyner Lucas, Laufey, LE SSERAFIM, Lojay, Morgan Wallen, Myke Towers, NCT Dream, Pheelz, Playboi Carti, RAYE and The Warning.\n\n'Fortnight'\n\nSwift's Post Malone collaboration \"Fortnight\" achieved particularly impressive renown.\n\nUnto itself, the song received eight nominations in the following categories:\n\nThe competitive voting for the Burger King-sponsored and vaunted \"Video of the Year\" Moonman trophy includes Ariana Grande's \"we can't be friends (wait for your love),\" Billie Eilish's \"LUNCH,\" Doja Cat's \"Paint The Town Red,\" Eminem's \"Houdini\" and SZA's \"Snooze.\"\n\nSwift's recent VMA history, can she attend the 2024 MTV VMAs?\n\nBarring any unforeseen schedule changes, it appears that Swift can attend the Video Music Awards on Sept. 10.\n\nThe date falls directly between the latest international and domestic legs of her Eras Tour.\n\nAug. 20 finds her finishing a five-night run at London's Wembley Stadium, while she returns to the road on Oct. 18 at Miami's Hard Rock Stadium.\n\nAt present, National Football League game dates for her beau, All-Pro Kansas City Chiefs tight end Travis Kelce, also do not prove problematic for her attendance.\n\nChiefs training camp runs until Aug. 15. The Sept. 10 date falls between a Sept. 5 matchup between the Chiefs and Baltimore Ravens and a Sept. 15 Chiefs versus Cincinnati Bengals matchup.\n\nAt 2023's festivities, Swift -- who went into the night with the most nominations -- was, with nine wins (including artist of the year, best pop, song of the year and video of the year), the most-awarded artist of the evening. Notably too, NSYNC had a surprise reunion just in time to present her with an award for best pop song.\n\nFor the second year in a row, Swift won video of the year. Twelve months prior, she won for \"All Too Well\" (10 Minute Version) (Taylor's Version).\n\n\"This is unbelievable. The fact that this is a fan-voted award means so much to me. It's really felt like the adventure of a lifetime this past year. I cannot believe that it was a year ago at the VMAs that I announced the 'Midnights' album. All I have to say tonight is thank you,\" Swift added.\n\nPost Malone's expanding influence\n\nPost Malone's nominations as both a country and pop artist are notable.\n\nYes, he's been nominated eight times alongside Taylor Swift for \"Fortnight.\"\n\nHowever, his radio, sales and streaming-beloved Morgan Wallen duet \"I Had Some Help\" was also nominated for Best Collaboration alongside his work on \"Fortnight,\" plus Drake, Sexyy Red and SZA' -'s \"Rich Baby Daddy,\" GloRilla and Megan Thee Stallion's \"Wanna Be,\" Jessie Murph and Jelly Roll's \"Wild Ones, plus Jung Kook and Latto's \"Seven.\"\n\nHis impressive 2024 run follows being nominated only once in 2022 and 2023 for his Doja Cat duet \"I Like You (A Happier Song)\" and work with The Weeknd for \"One Right Now.\"\n\nBEST Music Awards with 10 nominations | Connaught Telegraph", "body": "Taylor Swift leads pack for MTV Video Music Awards with 10 nominations RSS Syndicated Content Published: Tue 6 Aug 2024, 6:54 PM Last updated: Tue 6 Aug 2024, 7:10 PM\n\nBy Casey Cooper-Fiske, PA Entertainment Reporter\n\nTaylor Swift leads the pack for this year's MTV Video Music Awards (VMA) with 10 nominations.\n\nThe 34-year-old has been nominated eight times for Post Malone collaboration Fortnight, as well as for her body of work over the past year, in the best pop and artist of the year categories.\n\nCollaborator Malone, who has nine nominations, is close behind, with eight for Fortnight and another for best collaboration for I Had Some Help, recorded with Morgan Wallen.\n\nAriana Grande, Bad Bunny, Eminem, Sabrina Carpenter and SZA have also been nominated in the artist of the year category, alongside Swift.\n\nSwift and Malone's collaboration is joined by Billie Eilish, Doja Cat, Eminem, SZA and Ariana Grande in the race for video of the year.\n\nCompeting with Fortnight in the song of the year category are Carpenter, Teddy Swims, Jack Harlow, Beyonce and Kendrick Lamar.\n\nLast year's ceremony saw Swift take home nine awards, bringing her total number of VMA awards to 23.\n\nOnly Beyonce, with 28, has more awards, with Swift trailed by Madonna, who has 20 awards, and Lady Gaga, who has 19.\n\nOther musicians to see a high number of nominations include Grande, Carpenter and Eminem, who have six each, and Megan Thee Stallion and SZA, who have five each.\n\nChappell Roan, Gracie Abrams and Morgan Wallen are among the artists being recognised at the VMAs for the first time.\n\nVoting began online on Tuesday and will continue until Friday August 30, across 15 gender neutral categories.\n\nThe awards ceremony will take place at 1am on Wednesday September 10 at the UBS Arena in New York's Long Island.\n\nVoting in the best new artist category will continue during the show.\n\nRSS Syndicated {"uri": "2024-08-445934922", "lang": "eng", "isDuplicate": false, "date": "2024-08-06", "time": "16:09:19", "dateTime": "2024-08-06T16:09:19Z", "dateTimePub": "2024-08-06T16:00:00Z", "dataType": "news", "sim": 0.7098039388656616, "url": "https://variety.com/2024/music/awards/mtv-vmas-nominations-taylor-swift-post-malone-awards-1236096620/", "title": "Taylor Swift Leads MTV VMAs Nominations With 10, as Post Malone, Sabrina Carpenter, Ariana Grande and Eminem Also Get a Big Look", "body": "Aerosmith Announces Retirement From Touring, Saying Steven Tyler's 'Recovery From His Vocal Injury Is Not Possible' 4 days ago\n\nUnsurprisingly in a year in which she has dominated all other comers in recorded music and the live sphere, Taylor Swift emerged as the leading nominee for MTV's Video Music Awards, collecting 10 nominations in the competition for the 2024 spacemen.\n\nPost Malone followed close behind with nine nods, primarily for sharing Swift's \"Fortnight\" nominations, as her featured guest on that hit.\n\nSabrina Carpenter, Eminem and Ariana Grande tied for third place among VMAs finalists, with six nominations each. SZA and Megan Thee Stallion both picked up five nominations.\n\nMoving ahead in the contest with four nods each are Olivia Rodrigo, Teddy Swims and, making big inroads as a solo artist, Blackpink's Lisa. Tied with three nominations apiece are Benson Boone, Anitta, Dua Lipa, Tyla, Bleachers and GloRilla.\n\nThe VMAs will air live from UBS Arena on Sept. 10 at 8 p.m. ET/PT. It's the first time for the awards show to be based in that New York venue, after being settled in at New Jersey's Prudential Center for the last two years. A host has not yet been announced.\n\nFan voting in 15 categories, including video of the year, is open now through Aug. 30 at vote.mtv.com. But one category, best new artist, will leave voting open all the way through showtime on Sept. 10.\n\nSwift has won the top prize, the video of the year award, for the last two years running, and picked it up four times overall. If she wins again this year, for the \"Fortnight\" video, she will be the first artist to have a \"three-peat\" as well as the first to be a five-time winner in the category in VMAs history. She won a year ago for \"Anti-Hero\" and in 2022 for \"All Too Well: The Short Film\"; prior to those successive wins, Swift picked up the prize for \"You Need to Calm Down\" in 2019 and \"Bad Blood\" in 2015.\n\nIf anyone is wondering if the possibility exists for Swift to personally pick up any trophies that come her way, the answer is yes, since she will be taking a nearly three-month break from the Eras Tour beginning in late August. If Swift hasn't announced a release date for \"Reputation (Taylor's Version)\" by then, there may be a big tune-in among Swifties hopeful that she will use a VMAs speech to do it; there is some history there, as the singer announced her \"Midnights\" album at the 2022 ceremony.\n\nThe nominees for video of the year are Grande's \"We Can't Be Friends (Wait for Your Love),\" Eilish's \"Lunch,\" Doja Cat's \"Paint the Town Red,\" Eminem's \"Houdini,\" SZA's \"Snooze\" and the Swift/Malone collab \"Fortnight.\"\n\nIn the artist of the year category, Swift is joined by her tourmate, Carpenter, as well as Grande, Bad Bunny, Eminem and SZA. It's a notable achievement for Carpenter that she is being nominated for artist of the year in the first year she has received any VMAs nominations at all.\n\nSwift is the only artist to be nominated in the best direction category for directing her own video. Her other nominations came for artist of the year and -- all for \"Fortnight\" -- song of the year, best collaboration, best pop, best cinematography, best editing, best visual effects and best art direction.\n\nWith no album out of his own yet, Malone got his nine nominations by sharing most of Swift's nods, as the featured artist on \"Fortnight.\" Malone did pick up one nomination for a non-Swift song, as he is represented in the best collaboration category twice, getting a second nod there for \"I Had Some Help,\" the lead single off his forthcoming country album, on which he was joined by Morgan Wallen.\n\nThe currently hot Billie Eilish, Chappell Roan and Charli XCX have two nominations each, joined as double-nominees by Drake, Jelly Roll, Bad Bunny, Coldplay, Latto, Jung Kook, Usher, Victoria Monet, Tate McRae, Sexyy Red, Rauw Alejandro and Jessie Murph.\n\nBeyonc\u00e9, whose \"Cowboy Carter\" has been one of the year's most talked about albums, has one nomination, for \"Texas Hold 'Em\" as song of the year. Shaboozey, whose \"A Bar Song (Tipsy)\" has topped the Billboard Hot 100 for four nonconsecutive weeks so far, also has a single nod. In both cases, the artists released what were billed as \"visualizers,\" rather than the full produced music videos the VMAs typically honor.\n\nThe nominees for best new artist are Shaboozey, Boone, Roan, Swims, Tyla and Gracie Abrams.\n\nOther artists who picked up their first VMAs nominations ever, besides Carpenter, include Wallen, Alexander Stewart, Burna Boy, Coco Jones, Flyana Boss, Gunna, Joyner Lucas, Laufey, Le Sserafim, Lojay, Myke Towers, NCT Dream, Pheelz, Playboi Carti, Raye, Tyler Childers and the Warning. Many of those first-timers picked up their nominations through the category of MTV Push Performance of the Year, honoring everyone who was picked on a monthly basis for MTV's freshman artist initiative, or in the social-consciousness-honoring Video for Good division.\n\nTuesday's rollout includes all of the nominations except social categories, which MTV says will be revealed at a later date.\n\nThe telecast's executive producers are Bruce Gillmer and Den of Thieves co-founder Jesse Ignjatovic, with Barb Bialkowski as co-executive producer. Alicia Portugal and Jackie Barba are the executives in charge of production; Wendy Plaut is executive in charge of celebrity talent; and Lisa Lauricella is the show's music talent executive.\n\nAriana Grande - \"We Can't Be Friends (Wait for Your Love)\" - Republic Records\n\nBillie Eilish - \"Lunch\" - Darkroom / Interscope Records\n\nDoja Cat - \"Paint The Town Red\" - Kemosabe Records / RCA Records\n\nEminem - \"Houdini\" - Shady / Aftermath / Interscope Records\n\nSZA - \"Snooze\" - Top Dawg Entertainment / RCA Records\n\nTaylor Swift ft. Swift is also up for artist of the year, while the song also earned her a nomination for song of the year and best collaboration, with Post Malone.\n\nSpeaking of Malone, he's hot on Swift's heels, with nine nominations of his own. In addition to appearing in the best collaboration field with Swift, Malone is nominated for his hit \"I Had Some Help\" with Morgan Wallen.\n\nAriana Grande, Sabrina Carpenter and Eminem have six nominations apiece, while Megan Thee Stallion and SZA notched five each.\n\nThere are 29 first-time nominees, including such names as Wallen, Benson Boone, Chappell Roan, Gracie Abrams, Jelly Roll and Swims.\n\nFans can vote for their choices in 15 categories at MTV.com through Aug. 30, while voting for best new artist will stay open through Sept. 10. The artist behind \"Tortured Poets Society\" secured 10 noms, one more than the second most nominated artist, Post Malone.\n\nAltogether, Swift was nominated for Video of the Year, Artist of the Year, Song of the Year, Best Collaboration, Best Pop, Best Direction, Best Cinematography, Best Editing, Best Visual Effects and Best Art Direction. If Swift wins the coveted Video of the Year, she will shatter her own record and become the only artist to win the top honor three years in a row as well as five times throughout her career.\n\nSwift is nominated for Video of the Year for \"Fortnight,\" a song she collaborated on with Post Malone, who stands as the second most nominated artist this year. In addition to Video of the Year, \"Fortnight\" and Malone were nominated for Song of the Year, Best Collaboration, Best Direction, Best Cinematography, Best Editing, Best Visual Effects and Best Art Direction. Malone was nominated a second time for Best Collaboration thanks to \"I Had Some Help,\" his song featuring Morgan Wallen.\n\nAfter Swift and Post Malone, Ariana Grande, Eminem and Sabrina Carpenter were the most nominated, securing six honors each. Megan Thee Stallion and SZA were then nominated five times apiece. Finally, LISA, Olivia Rodrigo and Teddy Swims each secured four noms.\n\nCarpenter and Swims' multiple nominations are especially impressive because 2024 marks the first time both have been VMAs nominees. Altogether, there were 29 first-time nominees. Benson Boone and Tyla secured three honors apiece. As for the first-timers who were nominated in two categories, Chappell Roan, Jelly Roll, Jessie Murph, Rauw Alejandro, Sexyy Red and Victoria Mon\u00e9t all made that list.\n\nStarting today, fans will be able to vote for their favorite artists across the 15 gender-neutral categories. The voting window will close on Aug. 30 for Video of the Year, Best Collaboration and Artist of the Year. Voting for Best New Artists will be active until Sept. 10. Nominations for social categories will be announced at a later date.\n\nAfter two years in New Jersey, the VMAs are returning to New York for 2024. Kansas laureate Traci Brimhall, who hopes to bring chefs and poets together for a state community cookbook; and Angelika Brewer, poet laureate of Ogden, Utah, who is working on a local archive.\n\nOther Fellows include Maine laureate Julia Bouwsma, Colorado laureate Andrea Gibson and Joseph Rios, laureate of Fresno, California.\n\nThe fellowship program was made possible by the Mellon Foundation.\n\n\"These exceptional writers share the distinctive responsibility of advancing action, advocacy, and civic transformation in their communities through the power of poetry,\" said Mellon Foundation President Elizabeth Alexander. \"We at Mellon are pleased to provide them with the additional resources needed to carry out this mission, building further appreciation of and engagement with the written word across the United States.\"\n\nActor Akili McDowell is facing murder charges\n\nActor Akili McDowell, who starred in the television series \"David Makes Man\" and had roles in \"Billions\" and \"The Astronaut Wives Club,\" has been charged with fatally shooting a man in the parking lot of a Houston apartment complex, authorities said.\n\nMcDowell, 21, was charged last week with murder in the July 20 shooting death of Cesar Peralta, 20, the Harris County sheriff's office said. McDowell remained in jail Monday on $400,000 bond on the murder charge. The attorney listed for him in court records did not immediately reply to a request for comment.\n\n\"This is an unfortunate situation and I am in prayer for Akili and those impacted by this tragedy,\" said his manager, Jonell Whitt, adding that she had no further comment.\n\nThe sheriff's office said deputies found an unresponsive man with gunshot wounds after responding to a call about a shooting at an apartment complex on July 20. The sheriff's office said several witnesses told deputies the man had been in a physical altercation with another man, who fled on foot after the shooting.\n\n\"David Makes Man,\" which aired on Oprah
